E X P E D I T I O N S
4 . T H E D E V I L L I V E S
I N S T I L L W A T E R S
“In waking the tiger, use a long stick.”
— M A O T S E -T U N G
The PCs find a rare thing in the Far Spinward Colo-
nies—a society that, on the surface at least, is working
well. May Outpost KOI-610.01, was once a 3WE Royal
Marine outpost until it was taken over by the Chinese
Asian Nations Collective (CANC, page 17). Now,
the society is at war with itself and at odds with
the Xeno­morphs that inhabit the nearby ruins of an
ancient Engineer pyramid. The PCs must negotiate the
deadly forces at work, deal with the UPP, explore the
wonders of the pyramid and prevent the colony falling
into a full-blown insurrection.
W H AT I S G O I N G O N ?
May Outpost KOI-610.01 was once a 3WE Royal
Marine outpost, with—according to the Weyland
Corporation files—nearly a billion people in 2100.
This was a typo, the fat finger of an administrator
hitting “zero” too many times. The real figure
wasn’t even a million.
The colony survived the Isolation. Then, thirty
years ago, the Chinese Asian Nations Collective
arrived, fresh from the disaster that was their
home, Curzic Colony, begging for somewhere to
settle. Permission was given, but the relationship
was never friendly. Ten years ago, the CANC took
control. After a bitter struggle, their leader, Colonel
Zhāngjié, declared himself Warlord of the newly
formed “Great Kĕnéng Cooperative.” The Royal
Marines who surrendered were ruthlessly murdered,
and the rest fled into the wilderness to carry on
the fight.
Ten years later, seismic activity at the far east-
ern end of Xián Hú (literally “salty lake”) led to the
collapse of the cliff, revealing an ancient Engineer
pyramid, and rousing the Xeno­m orphs that were
sleeping there. Those who went to explore were
never seen again. Since then, on the three nights
of the spring and winter equinoxes, XX121LV bio-
luminescent Xeno­m orphs (page 138) leave the
pyramid to roam. They wreaked havoc in the colony
until Zhāngjié learned that leaving human sacrifices
would gain their attention, preventing further death
and destruction—except for their doomed sacri-
ficial victims, dragged away into the lake. These
victims were taken to feed the growing Hive in the
depths of the pyramid.
The pyramid was put off limits by Zhāngjié’s
order, and life went on. Then, a month ago, a scout
ship of the UPP Cosmos Exploration Corps arrived
under the command of Lt Colonel Victor Drubov.
Offering gifts of advanced tech with the promise
of more, Drubov tried to persuade the Cooperative
to join the UPP. Zhāngjié is not convinced but sees
these soldiers as his way to finally unearth the
pyramid’s secrets. The arrival of the PCs is another
golden opportunity for Zhāngjié to get what he
wants for the Cooperative, and to play them off
against the UPP.
219G A M E
M O T H E R
S E C T I O N
WHAT’S THE STORY, MOTHER?
The PCs receive a video call from Gaius aboard
UNCSS Ìyánlá
Ìyánlá..
“Your destination is May Outpost, designation
KOI-610.01. This is a Three World Empire military
base, first colonized in 2061 under the Weyland
Corporation then transferred to 3WE authority on
its establishment in 2088. The records suggest a
population of 900 million people in 2100—seems
a bit steep to me. The colony was not just a Royal
Marine base, it also had mining facilities to sup-
port an electronics production industry.
The planet is highly volcanic, with considerable
seismic activity and localized release of toxic
gasses, with a saline and caustic atmosphere.
Basic maintenance costs for May Outpost were
three times equivalent averages. It is also rather
warm, average daytime temperatures of 33 °C and
not dropping much lower at night. The year lasts
180 Earth days, and the day is 18 hours. At this
point in its cycle the planet should be approaching
the winter equinox.
That is May Outpost. It will be interesting to see
how accurate those 2100 reports are. Remember
you are exploring and seeking to understand
the current state of the colony and will offer
any humanitarian aid that may be required. If
a 3WE military authority still exists, you should
have little trouble re-incorporating them under
official authority. We will still need access to their
long data disc so we can assess their long-term
development, and I’m expecting the usual Colony
Potential Report: industrial output; trade oppor-
tunities; political set-up and stability; and any ad
hoc opportunities.
All the best, Solovetsky Island.”
C L U E S T O T H E M E TA P U Z Z L E
The PCs can learn the fourth clue of the campaign
(page 162) during this expedition, by exploring the
Engineer pyramid and deciphering the glyphs that
adorn the wall of the Shrine. They can also have the
first campaign clue (page 162) corroborated by
KOI-610.01
KOI-610.01 is an Earth-like volcanic planet, with daily
temperatures reaching 33 °C and not dropping much
lower at night. The air is breathable, but pockets of
toxic gas can emerge anywhere, along with the fre-
quent geysers and ground bursts. With so much toxic
gas and salt-blown particles in the air, corrosion is a
constant problem. For every Shift that a mechanical
device (including spaceships and pressure suits) is
exposed to the weather roll a Stress Die—on
it
malfunctions either immediately or when next used.
To repair it takes a HEAVY MACHINERY roll and a
Turn of work. The planet is severely tilted on its axis,
bringing extreme seasons in its 180-day year. When
the PCs arrive, it’s the winter equinox at May Out-
post, with equal hours of daylight and night and the
weather is stormy and wet.
The planetary map gives you all the details
you need for KOI-610.01 should your PCs want to
further explore or even colonize it, using the rules
in the Appendix: Building Your Own Better World
(page 275).

Warlord Zhāngjié—if asked he will say there is a band
of pirates called Gorham’s Marauders who attack ships
to wipe their navigation data, but they don’t dare raid
the Great Kĕnéng Cooperative.

KICKING OFF THE ACTION
As the PCs approach the planet, their scans reveal
the following: the planet is volatile with high levels of
volcanic gasses in the upper atmosphere; there’s lots
of radio chatter—the signal that a living settlement
still persists; and pockets of twinkling civilization link
together around a central town by a lake that shim-
mers with a bluey-white glow.
Then the comms unit crackles, and a message first
in Chinese, then English:
“Unidentified vessel, this is the Great Kĕnéng Coop-
erative Orbital Authority. Identify yourself and state
your destination and purpose. Be warned, any act
deemed aggressive, hostile, or non-conforming with
instructions will be met with relentless defensive force.
Respond.”
Unless the PCs say or do something to anger the
Orbital Authority, they will be instructed to land at
the Landing Strip. Landing requires a PILOT test with
a +1 modification, thanks to the support of the ground
crew. A failed roll means the ship has landed heavily,
taking D3 points of damage.
As the PCs make their approach, they see the
layout of the town, built up at the western end of
the briny lake. All roads lead away, snaking into the
distance where much smaller settlements can be seen.
On the north-east shore of the lake lies what must
have been an old settlement, now derelict and ruined.
It sits adjacent to a large cliff that forms the east end
of the lake. Part of the cliff has fallen away leaving
exposed an awe-inspiring relic, once buried beneath
the earth. It looks like a pyramid set into the rock, one
side of which has been sheared away by the landslide.

M O T H E R
S E C T I O N
S H O R E PA R T Y : As the Solovetsky Island’s negotia-

to join the shore party. Once the UPP’s presence is
revealed she will take a very hard line with the Coop-
erative in negotiations, and cause Zhāngjié to lose
patience with her and the PCs.
O N T H E G R O U N D : Assuming the PCs comply
with these instructions to land they will be met by a
group of ten armed guards (page 171) under the
command of Captain Guanting. She will politely but
firmly invite them to a meeting with Warlord Zhāng-
jié, as they are clearly important visitors. Weapons
are not allowed. If they agree they will be escorted
in an open-topped personnel carrier to the War-
lord’s compound. As they rumble through the colony,
the PCs cannot fail to notice the frequent guard
checkpoints with five or six well-armed soldiers.
They can learn more with a group OBSERVATION roll:

clothing and looking well fed, no obvious signs of
poverty or destitution, and building work is com-
petent if not fancy. But few people are smiling,
while at the same time none are showing obvious
signs of unhappiness either. They seem docile.
TWO OR MORE

CAPTAIN G UANTIN G
Honorable and professional, Guanting is especially
loyal towards Brigadier Xìn Wŏ, as she fears Warlord
Zhāngjié’s brutal nature and arbitrary temper. She takes
her job seriously and will do everything in her power to
prevent harm coming to the PCs while they are under
her protection. She wants the insurrection to end, but
believes negotiation is the way to assure that, not
repression and violence.

Honorable, insightful and with a great sense of fair
play, Xìn Wŏ is Warlord Zhāngjié’s right hand. An
expert combat leader, she holds the loyalty of the
troops. Since the UPP arrived, she’s been having ever
greater reservations about them. Their methods have
no dignity or honor, something she quietly loathes. She
agrees with Zhāngjié that power through strength is
the best way to build a secure community, but it must
be honorable, even if she and the Warlord have not
always lived up to that ideal.
She wants to ensure power remains with the Coop-
erative, so they can negotiate the best deal for their
people from the newcomers, and not be strong-armed
by these UPP barbarians.

M AY O U T P O S T
May Outpost is built of stone and metal, crowded
buildings and narrow streets filled with subdued
people, keeping their heads down to avoid the interest
of the Warlord’s Guard.
WA R L O R D ’ S C O M P O U N D : Ringed by a 5-meter-
high stone wall with an imposing wrought iron gate,
the compound contains a luxurious palace with
gardens and pools as well as a garden atelier where
Zhāngjié holds court. There are always two or three
guards within a zone of the PCs.
B A R R A C K S : Housing 200 soldiers and their equip-
ment, training facilities and vehicles, the three build-

YŎ U Y Ì S À I B A R R A C K S : Ostensibly built as
another barracks, everyone knows this houses the
underground prison of the Kĕnéng Cooperative. Sev-
eral hundred political prisoners are held here. A ballot
is held at every equinox to choose six of them as
sacrifices for the Xeno­morphs, two per night over the
three nights.

R I V E R S : Three rivers flow out of Xián Hú: the Xīn
Tàiwùshì Hé (“New Thames”), the Xīn Sāi Wēn (“New
Severn”) and Xīn Chángjiāng (“New Yangtze”). Of
these, only the Xīn Tàiwùshì Hé can be crossed easily
without a bridge. The other rivers are so swift that
a MOBILITY roll is needed. If the roll is failed, the
PC is swept away by the current and needs another
MOBILITY check each Round, as a fast action, to avoid
drowning.

pipes, valves, and towers, that provides all the clean
water for the nearby town.
WA R E H O U S E S : Piled high with useful resources:
minerals, ore, raw materials, surplus food, construction
equipment, emergency settlement kits.

STAN LEY S H EP PARD
Intrepid, eager but ruthless, Sheppard is the Speaker
for the Union Mutual Society, and covertly a leader of
the 3WE insurrectionists. He’s not an unreasonable
man, and while he would admit that general living stan-
dards under Zhāngjié have improved, he cannot forget
at what cost—kidnappings, murder, and sacrifices.
His network knows of the UPP visitors (he hasn’t heard
the term “UPP” and wouldn’t understand it if he did).
Despite the risk to himself he is desperate to meet the
PCs and get their help (see the events The Insurrection-
ist’s Message and The Raid).
STRENGTH 4, AGILITY 3, WITS 4, EMPATHY 4
HEALTH: 4
SKILLS: Close Combat 2, Ranged Combat 2,
Stamina 2, Observation 3, Command 3
TALENT: Subdue, Hard Hitter

R U I N E D O L D T O W N : Formerly the site of the
Royal Marines garrison and the town that grew around
it, the entire settlement was destroyed during the war
with the CANC. Now it is a dusty, salty, desolate ruin.
E X E C U T I O N A L L E Y : The site where the last of
the marines, those who surrendered, were lined up
and executed. Their desiccated bodies lie where they
fell, deliberately left as a reminder of Warlord Zhāng-
jié’s brutality. +1 STRESS LEVEL to those witnessing
the scene.
E X P E D I T I O N S
O L D R OYA L M A R I N E B U N K E R : The entrance is
through a disused sewage overflow pipe in the south-
east of town. If it is being searched for a successful
OBSERVATION roll will find it, with a +3 modification if
the PCs have been given directions to find it. A ladder
goes down 30 meters to a small complex of five rooms
off a central chamber. There is no power, but the air
is good and it is warm. Captain Snell and five marines
are here—they will defend themselves unless the PCs
make it clear they are friends.
CAPTAIN HAN NAH S N ELL
Resilient, obsessive, with only one thing to live for—to
take revenge against Warlord Zhāngjié. Ten years ago,
when the defeat of the remaining marines was inevita-
ble, Snell’s commanding officer ordered her to take her
unit and flee, to set up as partisans and continue the
fight. This she did with a heavy heart. Since then, the
16 surviving marines under her command have been a
thorn in the side of the CANC, but never able to force
an uprising, even with the resistance network.
She knows some important visitors have arrived (the
UPP scouts) and is planning a raid to assassinate them.
For now, she has returned to the old Royal Marine
bunker in the Old Town, to await intelligence from
Sheppard and the resistance.

THE PYRAMID
Hidden for centuries, the pyramid still has enough
residual power to illuminate its interior with an eerie
blue glow that seems to come from nowhere, just
bright enough to see, but not bright enough to banish
the shadows. The air inside is salty, and sound echoes
a very long way. The Main Level is flooded by the lake
to a depth of 1 meter, and the Cistern, with the excep-
tion of the rear vestibule and the Hive, is submerged.
227G A M E
M O T H E R
S E C T I O N
E N T R A N C E : A low and wide opening narrows as it
goes deeper, eventually revealing the deep shaft and
the down ramp. The Shaft goes directly to the Shrine,
200 meters below, but its walls are sheer. Any attempt
to climb down brings a −2 modification to MOBILITY
rolls, and one roll is needed for each 100 meters
traversed, which also takes one Turn. The down ramp
is wide enough to take a vehicle as large as a Daihotai
8×8 and spirals down to the Shrine.
S H R I N E : The Shrine is flooded to 1 meter deep. The
path that leads down to the Cistern is not immediately
visible, requiring an OBSERVATION roll to spot it (or
the PCs might stumble across it). On either side of the
Shrine are Engineer murals, covered in glyphs—the
fourth campaign clue (page 162). The glyphs can be
recorded and deciphered, with an OBSERVATION roll
with a –1 modification, otherwise DA/UT/UR on the
UNCSS Solovetsky Island can help.
C AV E R N O U S C H A M B E R S : One of the four cav-
ernous chambers was damaged by the earthquake and
landslide that revealed the pyramid in the first place
and is open and exposed to the waters of the lake.
All are flooded. They are huge, sounds echoing off
vaulted ceilings to roll around the space.
O V O I D C H A M B E R S : Nineteen of these chambers
are intact. However, two were damaged by the earth-
quake and landslide that revealed the pyramid in the
first place and are open and exposed to the waters of
the lake. All these chambers are flooded to 1m depth.
Roll D6 on the table below when the PCs explore each
chamber.
T H E C I S T E R N : An enormous open chamber, 500
meters across, and completely submerged. Visibility is
down to LONG range with a flashlight, MEDIUM range
without. At the western end, there is a runoff tunnel
that leads out into Xián Hú. At the eastern end, there is
a tunnel that leads upwards towards a source of blue
light that the PCs can make out through the gloom. It
leads the PCs into the vestibule and the hive.
T H E H I V E : The tunnel leads up into a large chamber
with a pocket of trapped air. It’s breathable. In the
center of the chamber is a raised dais—the center of the
new hive. The Xeno­morphs have brought their victims
here and are turning them into Ovomorphs, while they
protect the Royal Egg at the center, just waiting for the
right time to rear the Queen. There are two XX121LV
Xeno­morphs here, currently in PASSIVE mode but if
disturbed they will attack and add the PCs to their
hive—read The Nascent Hive sidebar to your players.

THE NASCENT HIVE
The dais is 30 meters wide, a dull metallic but
stone-like material crisscrossed with electric blue
slashes, giving off an intensely bright light. Sitting
atop this is a grisly sight. What appears to be the
deformed bodies of people, maybe as many as 50,
lie in concentric circles. They appear to be losing
limbs as they are impossibly absorbed back into
their growing flesh, skin thickening, some more
deformed than others. In the center of all this
twisted humanity rests a large leathery object, in
pride of place, with two of those glowing devils,
just like those that arose from the water to snatch
the poor sacrificial victims, almost cuddled
around it. All is quiet. All appears dormant and
dead, until one of the mutating people moves
and lets out a deep and hopeless groan. Everyone
gains +1 STRESS LEVEL .
EVENTS
T H E I N S U R R E C T I O N I S T ’ S M E S S A G E : Stanley
Sheppard needs to get a message to the PCs and
arranges a diversion. As the PCs travel in the town,
they see two vehicles crash and suddenly an argument
breaks out. Within seconds, a shouting crowd has
gathered, and everyone is being buffeted. The PCs’
guards aggressively try to keep the people away, but
in the crush a random PC suddenly feels a note thrust
into their hand and has a moment’s eye contact with a
young woman before she disappears into the throng.
The note says: “Things are not as they seem. You may
be in danger. Find me at the Three Lions. Don’t bring
your guards.” If the PCs follow this up, they will find
Sheppard waiting for them.
A D R E A D F U L S A C R I F I C E : Early in the expedi-
tion, the PCs will be approached by Captain Guanting,
who tells them the Warlord requests their presence at
a special event. They are escorted to the Gallows and
directed to a small platform 30 meters from the water,
to join Zhāngjié and Wŏ. From here they can observe
what Zhāngjié calls “a special ritual”. A crowd gathers
along a low metal fence to watch. Shortly afterwards,
a Daihotai 8×8 appears, a man and a woman are
dragged out by four soldiers and chained to the posts
near the lake’s edge. Zhāngjié explains this is the first
of three days of sacrifice and these criminals drew the
short straws.
Unless the PCs take some action, they will see the
water at the shore’s edge glow, and two luminous
XX121LV Xeno­morphs (page 138) crawl from the
lake. The victims beg to be reprieved, and some in the
crowd shout for mercy. The PCs gain +1 STRESS LEVEL .
Unless the PCs intervene, the victims will be torn from
their chains and carried away into the water. If they
do intervene, the Xeno­morphs will fight back, but will
retreat rather than fight to the death. The crowd will
23 0
panic and guards will surround Zhāngjié to protect
him. Zhāngjié will command them to stop, Wŏ will
quietly approve, but the guards won’t intervene until
the action is over. If the PCs disobey him, Zhāngjié
will be furious, storming off with his guards, and their
relationship will be badly damaged. At your discretion
this can trigger the event Aggressive Negotiations.
S H A K E M E A L L N I G H T L O N G : An earthquake
suddenly strikes, and the world jags back and forth, up
and down. Everyone must make a MOBILITY roll or fall
prone, and then a MOBILITY roll is required to stand
again. They may take damage from falling debris. The
quake lasts D6 Rounds and may provide excellent
cover for the PCs to slip away from their guards.
T H E AT TA C K : As the PCs travel in the town, a group
of five insurrectionists (page 171) launch an attack
against a roadblock. Two CANC guards are gunned
down without a chance, and the other three are hit
but try to fight back. The PCs are protected by two of
their guards, who try to hustle them into cover, while
Guanting and the other three join the fight against the
insurrectionists. The PCs can help the CANC or use
this as a chance to slip away from their guards.
T H E R A I D : Play this event if the PCs have managed
to slip away from their guards to see the resistance
or Royal Marines. A young man acting as a lookout
rushes into their meeting, breathless, and gasps: “The
guards are coming!” Three Rounds later, eight Cooper-
ative soldiers (page 171) carrying shock sticks and
modern AK-4047s burst into the scene from all sides
and try to arrest everyone. If the PCs are arrested, they
are taken before Zhāngjié and interrogated over their
behavior (see the event Aggressive Negotiations).1 0 .

hot springs. A geyser builds near the PCs. They see a
sudden bubbling and frothing of the surface, and one
Round later a huge stream of steaming water bursts
into the air, that lasts for three Rounds. Anyone within
SHORT range takes an eight Base Dice attack, Damage
1, armor applies. Up to MEDIUM range, all are soaked
with hot water.pyramid for Zhāngjié. The PCs either witness them

R O T T E N E G G S : A pocket of sulfur dioxide bursts
from the ground and the air in the PCs’ zone is
suddenly saturated with it. They cannot mistake the
smell. Anyone breathing it will immediately suffer
from Extreme hypoxia (page 91). The pocket will
disperse in D6 Rounds in the open but will persist for
D6 Turns in an enclosed space.S A B O TA G E : A huge explosion rocks the ground and

The water plant has been destroyed by Captain Snell

on the Xīn Sāi Wēn river rush to the scene, only to be

A G G R E S S I V E N E G O T I AT I O N S : If the PCs
anger Zhāngjié, he will insist they make reparations (to
advance Zhāngjié’s objectives). He will keep Lakota
Monroe at his compound for her safety and so negotia-
tions can progress with alacrity, but she is really a pris-

Brigadier Wŏ disapproves and advises Zhāngjié to treat

this as leverage to get the PCs to help, either to capture
the resistance fighters, or to explore the pyramid.
I P R E D I C T A R I O T : All day people have been
gathering in Huánghòu Square. Suddenly, as if on
a command, they start to riot, surging through the
streets of the Zuì Hăo De District towards the War-
lord’s Compound, smashing and destroying as they go.
CANC soldiers pour from the barracks in an attempt
to stop the rioting, but the whole area descends into
chaos. The PCs witness a group capture three of
the colony “elite,” and push them into an alley. The
three will be lynched before the PCs’ eyes unless they
intervene.
T H E U P P G O F O R T H E P R I Z E : Colonel
Drubov and his squad leave the town to explore the
LIEUTENANT CO LO N EL VICTO R D R U BOV
UPP COSMOS EXPLORATION CORPS
Honorable, ambitious but with a powerful sense of
self-preservation, Drubov has found dealing with
Zhāngjié difficult—not least because Drubov isn’t a
politician and Zhāngjié, as a former Colonel and now
warlord, thinks he outranks him. And this despite the
gifts of modern armor and weapons. Drubov is desper-
ate to get this outpost to sign on the dotted line as a
member of the UPP before the PCs arrive. If he and his
squad of five troopers and one Davydovich android
have to investigate the pyramid as Zhāngjié’s price,
then so be it. If not, Drubov is not above a palace
coup, killing the warlord and replacing him with his
second in command, Wŏ.
If the PCs save Drubov’s life in the pyramid, he will
feel a strong sense of obligation to them. He will tell
them to beware, as all is not as it seems on the Great
Mother Mission. He won’t say any more unless the PCs
succeed at a MANIPULATION roll, in which case he will
add that some colonists may be more than they seem
(referring to the SOF troops in hypersleep aboard the
UNCSS Ìyánlá

FINALE
Tensions come to a head and the insurrectionists start
a vicious uprising. The Royal Marine partisans launch
an attack on the Intelligence HQ, while elsewhere
across the city bands of resistance fighters arm them-
selves and take the fight to the CANC.
Zhāngjié will call the troops out and issue an order
that anyone on the streets must be shot on sight. Wŏ
is very worried that this will bring about a needless
bloodbath and tries to convince Zhāngjié that if they
can repel the attack on the Intelligence HQ this will
be enough to quell the uprising, and then they can
negotiate a settlement. Zhāngjié will see this as a sign
of weakness and disloyalty. How this confrontation
plays out should be down to the PCs’ actions and who
they support.
The PCs have several options: they can join the
fight on the CANC’s side, supporting either Zhāngjié’s
or Wŏ’s approach; they can join the fight on the side
of the insurrectionists; they can attempt to bring calm,
stop the fighting, and broker a peace; or they can get
the hell out of there until the carnage dies down. How
the uprising pans out, and who wins, is up to you as
GM, but obviously the PCs’ actions should influence
the outcome.
EPILOGUE
Warlord Zhāngjié or Brigadier Wŏ may offer the PCs
a reward if they would keep the Cooperative’s best
interests at heart when they return to the Great Mother
Mission, or in return for delivering supplies that the UN
won’t—like weapons. Governor Abantu could propose
a mission to wipe out the Xeno­morph hive, but the
PCs are offered a job by a corporate interest—get in
and get a specimen before the Governor has them all
exterminated. ■

E X P E D I T I O N S
A G A I N S T A S E A
O F T R O U B L E S
“It is in our nature to explore, to reach out into the unknown.
The only true failure would be not to explore at all.”
—ERNEST SHACKLETON
The PCs are ordered to search for the missing ship
UNCSS Typhoon, sent to survey two moons of the
gas giant KOI-2702.07, called Azizo and Arzu. They
intercept the Typhoon dead in space, its crew missing
after the Perfected tried to capture it. They trace its
path back to the two moons, to find one swamped by
the Perfected’s living Proto-Hive. They must explore a
derelict Engineer Juggernaut and confront the Per-
fected, to save the Typhoon’s crew, and escape alive
to raise the alarm.
W H AT I S G O I N G O N ?
The UNCSS Typhoon, under Captain Leland Barton,
was ordered to the KOI-2702 system, to survey the
moons of the seventh planet, a gas giant designated
KOI-2702.07, called Palmyra. Amongst the dozens
of tiny, rocky moons Palmyra has two of note—Azizo
and Arzu. Azizo is a small watery world, so far
untouched by any hands. Arzu, however, was an
Engineer outpost attacked by the Perfected many
thousands of years ago. Preferring death to infection,
many Engineers committed suicide. But some were
too late and became Perfected themselves.
Millennia passed, and the Perfected infection, the
Proto-Hive, on Arzu slowly spread across the planet
while the Perfected themselves slumbered—until
the Typhoon arrived and disturbed them. Too late
did Barton and his crew realize what was hap-
pening. Their ship was infected by the Proto-Hive
even as it fled. All the crew bar one escaped in the
two lifeboats, one—with Captain Barton and five
crew—launching quickly and falling back to Arzu, the
other—with three crew, including Barton’s wife, Anne
Bowers—launching later, and managing to reach
Azizo before it crashed.
The one crew member who was left aboard the
Typhoon, Alice Dudgeon (the sister of the UNCSS
Solovetsky Island’s pilot, Andi Dudgeon), could not
let the Typhoon fall into the hands of these monsters.
She overloaded the reactor and flooded the ship
with radiation, killing the Perfected and Children of
the Two Divines, and sacrificing herself. However,
the radiation only fed the growing Proto-Hive that
spread through the ship, and warped the positronic
brains of the vessel’s Working Joe androids, who are
now hostile.
On Azizo, three crew survived the crash, and await
rescue. On Arzu, however, the lifeboat with Captain
Barton and the other survivors was found by the
Perfected. While some resisted—two of whom were
killed by the Perfected—Barton was infected and
became one of them, a Stage I Abomination Patho-
gen Carrier (page 123). They were taken to the
Engineer Juggernaut, the Perfected’s base on Arzu.
Having failed in the attempt to capture the Typhoon,
they send a distress beacon from the lifeboat, hoping
to draw another ship to them, and lay the trail to the
Lychgate, the honey trap that will secure their pas-
sage to the Middle Heavens.
233G A M E
M O T H E R
S E C T I O N
WHAT’S THE STORY, MOTHER?
The PCs receive an unscheduled video call from
Gaius aboard UNCSS Ìyánlá
Ìyánlá..
“I’m sad to report that we have lost contact with
your sister ship, UNCSS Typhoon, under Captain
Leland Barton. They had been ordered to survey
KOI-2702.07, a gas giant with two moons possibly
suitable for colonization. I am sending a Throop
rescue ship but you are the closest vessel by sev-
eral days. Your orders are to proceed there imme-
diately, find and assist the Typhoon and her crew
should they need help, then complete the surveys
of the two moons. I assume you understand?
The moons are called Azizo and Arzu. From the
preliminary scans Azizo is a sub-Earth sized planet,
probably low G, with significant surface water.
Arzu on the other hand is a super-Earth, likely to
have high G and seems much drier. Colonization
recommendations for both, please.
Good luck Solovetsky Island, and give my
regards to Captain Barton when you find him.”
C L U E S T O T H E M E TA P U Z Z L E
The PCs can learn the fifth campaign clue during
this expedition, by reaching the Navigator Orrery on
the Engineer Juggernaut and witnessing the orrery
display.
KICKING OFF THE ACTION
The action starts with the PCs heading in the direction
of KOI-2702. As soon as they drop out of FTL, they
detect the transponder of the UNCSS Typhoon. It
has a minimal level of power, but is drifting, both its
lifeboats are missing, and it is emitting Weak radiation.
Any attempt to communicate is met with silence.
As a Magellan-class J SEV, the layout of the Typhoon is
identical to that of the Solovetsky Island (page 153).
The Typhoon’s crew are all fitted with Personal Data
Transmitters (PDTs). A successful COMTECH roll will
only detect Alice Dudgeon’s tracker on board, and her
life signs are very weak.
S H O R E PA R T Y : The ship’s pilot, Andi Dudgeon,
insists he joins as Alice Dudgeon is his younger
sister—he is distraught and desperate to save her. As
the expedition progresses, he will have a burning
desire for vengeance against those who attacked his
sister. As the Typhoon is drifting, Davor Koblenz, the
Solovetsky Island’s mechanic (page 159), suggests
he also should join the boarding party.
UNCSS TYPHOON
The Typhoon’s DA/UT/UR has been destroyed by the
radiation, along with many other systems, although
the basics of life support and emergency power still
work. The ship’s Working Joes (page 172), nick-
named Jake and Elwood by the crew, have suffered
severe damage to their programming. They are now
23 4
intensely protective of their ship and hostile to anyone
that boards it—see the event Don’t Ignore the Joes.
The residual radioactive effects can be felt as Weak
radiation (page 110 of the core rulebook) on board
the ship.1 0 .
E N G I N E CO N T R O L A N D T H E R E AC TO R :
The doors to this area have been sealed shut from
the inside, by Alice Dudgeon, and require a HEAVY
MACHINERY roll and a Turn of work to open. If this
fails, they can use a breaching charge from the
Solovetsky Island’s stores to blow it open. The reac-
tor is active but not running at full capacity, and its
radiation protections have been deactivated. These
can be restored with a HEAVY MACHINERY roll and
a Shift of work. Any attempt to fire up the ship’s
engines before then increases the radiation released
to Strong radiation, and use of FTL brings Extreme
radiation.
Alice Dudgeon is here, unconscious. She is
scorched and withered, and very close to death.
When the PCs find her, she needs to be stabilized
with a MEDICAL AID roll with a −2 modification, or she
will die. If this fails, her only chance is to get to the
medbay aboard the Solovetsky Island within one Turn.
To increase the tension of this race to save her life,
Andi Dudgeon will get angry or break down during
the rescue.
The engineering log shows that Dudgeon deliber-
ately removed the safety protocols for the Typhoon’s
reactor and flooded the ship with Extreme radiation
for one Turn.
E X P E D I T I O N S
B R I D G E : There are two Perfected (see the sidebar
The Dead Perfected), and five devotees here, all killed
by intense radiation sickness. They had been trying to
access the nav computer when they died. The scene is
grim, and all seeing it gain +1 STRESS LEVEL .
A check of the Typhoon’s last log entry shows the
ship arrived safely in the KOI-2702 system, proceeded
to survey the gas giant Palmyra and her moons before
inserting into orbit around Arzu. A COMTECH roll will
allow the PCs to see that the ship’s trajectory is a
straight line away from the gas giant.
D E C K C : The Proto-Hive (page 129) has grown
such that it has covered all of Deck C, with a Pro-
to-Hive Node (page 130) in every zone. Its tendrils
are working their way to Deck B, entwining around
the mesh walkways that are above, and look down
into, the cargo bay on Deck C. While the Nodes and
tendrils could be burned away using an incinerator,
the Proto-Hive has already merged with the ship
at the molecular level. The PCs will have to brave
the Proto-Hive and its Nodes if they want to access
this deck.
E Q U I P M E N T S T O R E S : The Typhoon has the same
stores aboard, in its various storage rooms, as the
Solovetsky Island. These can be found by the PCs, at
your discretion.
THE DEAD PERFECTED
Despite the scars of the intense radiation sick-
ness that killed them, the genderless Perfected
appear serene and majestic, their lithe forms a
little too long, their bodies just a little out of
proportion. Their silver-gray skin lies taught overa biomechanical series of tube-like bulges and
protrusions, almost an extra dark skeleton. If the
PCs choose to autopsy either of them, they will
find their anatomy is nothing like that of a human,
and seems random and disordered.
THE DOOMED TYPHOON
Alice Dudgeon used the reactor’s radiation to
kill the Perfected that boarded the ship, and the
Children of the Two Divines who came with them,
before they could extract the navigation data for
the Middle Heavens from the Typhoon’s computer.
However, while this killed these enemies, it only
nourished the living Proto-Hive that infected theship. The entire ship will become a Proto-Hive
within two Shifts, unless the PCs stop it by over-
loading the reactor with a HEAVY MACHINERY roll
and self-destructing the Typhoon (which would
happen one Turn later), but Jake and Elwood, the
ship’s Working Joes (page 172) will try to pre-
vent this.

T H E T WO M O O N S O F PA L M Y R A
A Z I Z O : Azizo is a watery world of great seas and
lakes, with a scattering of island archipelagos. Vol-
canically active, frequent eruptions pump a fine dust
of iron oxide into the air, giving the high atmosphere
a red, hazy tinge. The planet is cool—temperatures
never rise much above 12 °C or below 5 °C, except at
the poles. The gravity is 0.5G, causing gravity dys-
praxia (page 91).hovers just above freezing, except at the poles where
it falls much lower. Gravity is double that of Earth—the
PCs may suffer from gravity dyspraxia (page 91).
As these planets are moons of a gas giant their day
length is eccentric. The reflection from Palmyra illu-
minates the moons as well as the red glow from their
giant star. For half their orbital periods the moons
never get darker than twilight.
A R Z U : Arzu is a cold and heavy super-Earth, with a
dense atmosphere and little liquid water on its surface.
Mountainous and riven with crevasses and canyons, it
presents a challenging environment. The temperatureA R R I VA L : When the PCs arrive in the vicinity of Pal-
myra, they can detect the distress signal from Lifeboat
One, coming from the northern hemisphere of Azizo.
AZIZO
Azizo is a pristine planet, an excellent candidate
for colonization, should the PCs wish to explore
this option.
The lifeboat has landed in the northern hemi-
sphere (Northern Hemisphere West on the planet
map), and the PCs can home in on it. They can
detect the PDT traces of the remaining crew with
a COMTECH roll:
Security Officer Anne Bowers—alive, the wife of
Captain Leland Barton
Pilot Anka Karsen—alive, but weak life signs

archipelago of a vast sea, with thousands of tiny
islands and lagoons, and have been steadily sur-
rounded by slow-moving plant life that is infested
with huge insects that are highly aggressive if
disturbed. They are trapped.
L A N D FA L L : The closest island big enough to
land the ship is 15 km from the lifeboat, but the PCs
have amphibious Daihotai 8×8 tractors aboard the
Solovetsky Island to cover the distance. Landing is
difficult, with a −1 modification to the PILOTING roll.
A failed roll causes D3 Damage.

ARZU
Arzu was once an Engineer staging post, a hub for
vessels traveling across this sector of space. As such it
was an obvious place for the Perfected to concentrate
their efforts, in the hope of taking control and infecting
ships as they passed through. The Engineer facilities
were concentrated in the northern hemisphere, now lost
under the Perfected’s living Proto-Hive.
Lifeboat Two landed in a ravine within the equatorial
region, three kilometers south of the leading edge of
the Proto-Hive infection. Here, the hive has consumed
a number of Engineer Juggernauts that now litter the
landscape as huge mounds of earth and seething Pro-
to-Hive matter. At the edge of this dreadful landscape
there is a partially consumed Engineer Juggernaut,
covered in Proto-Hive tendrils, plant matter and earth.
Its two enormous prongs are simply bulges under the
earth, but the flat end of the ship remains exposed.
The lifeboat’s emergency beacon is active but weak,
and once the PCs are in orbit they can home in on it.
Once within 20 km, a COMTECH roll will detect weak
PDT traces of the remaining crew—these are too weak
to pinpoint their exact location but can track them to
within about 100 m:
Captain Leland Barton—alive, located three km north
of the lifeboat
Counselor Gráinne Shields—alive, located with
the captain
Security Officer Azad Rukmini—alive, located with
the captain
Navigator Petronella Edouard—deceased, at the
lifeboat
Prospector Sargis Narene—deceased, at the lifeboat
Scientist Ji-Hye Suk—deceased, at the lifeboat.

THE HONEY TRAP
The Perfected have lost their patience with the Chil-
dren of the Two Divines and their failure to acquire a
ship that can take them to the Middle Heavens. They
have decided to allow the humans to learn of their
false plan to use the Engineer Lychgate to make that
journey. This is the honey trap—the lure to bring the
humans to the Lychgate, where the Perfected will
spring their surprise and capture all the ships they
need. But they can’t make it seem too easy—can’t
just give the humans the data—for they must not
smell a rat. After all, only one of the PCs needs to
make it back with the information.
L I F E B OAT T W O
This has the same layout as Lifeboat One.
The main airlock door stands open, and the power
is on. The lifeboat has been badly damaged by its
emergency landing and inside is a shambles. There are
few supplies left scattered among the debris, but the
MedPods still work. Communications are dead, except
for the automated emergency beacon.
Outside the lifeboat, tracks lead north, towards a
rising ridge of earth covered in plant growth and the
gray-black-crimson of the Proto-Hive. If the PCs check,
and succeed with an OBSERVATION roll, they can
see there are eight sets of tracks heading north (the

F O O D S T O R E S : The bodies of Sargis Narene and

LOWER LEVEL
This ship has been here for thousands of years.
The Engineers who were intending to flee from
the Perfected realized they could not escape
infection and chose to sacrifice themselves
rather than risk spreading the plague further.
Over the millennia, the Engineer ship has cor-
roded and worn away, only a shell of it remaining
underneath the earth and Proto-Hive matter. All
the tunnels have tendrils running through them,
and there is a Nodule in every zone (page 130).AT R I U M C AV E R N : A cavern formed by years of
matter accumulating around the decaying ship, held
in place by the Proto-Hive. On all sides the walls are
recognizable as the outer shell of an Engineer Jugger-
naut. Where the hull has fallen away, mounds of debris
have gathered. To the north end, the Proto-Hive
matter continues to encroach, filling the space.
The cavern is only illuminated by a fire in the
middle, that casts a weak orange glow. Three figures
sit around it—two devotees and Azad Rukmini. Ruk-
mini has been separated from the other survivors as
he chose not to join the Perfected.
A P E R T U R E S : These oval openings are five
meters wide. None appear to have any kind of
door or bulkhead. Those on the lower level can
be accessed with a bit of nimble footwork, but
those on the upper level are 20 meters off the
ground and require a MOBILITY roll with a −2
modification to access. The successful use of an
ASSO-400 Harpoon Gun or similar equipment
will remove that negative modifier.R E A DY R O O M : Full of racks that reach from floor
to ceiling, this area is a warren of twisted structures
and ornate scaffolding. Captain Barton and Gráinne
Shields are here, guarded by Mother Ma’Kayla (page
144), four devotees, and two Stage IV Aethon
XX033 Deacons (page 135). They are waiting for
the PCs to arrive and for the Perfected to make their
move but will challenge the PCs if they come here.1 0 .
E X P E D I T I O N S
C A R G O 1 : These long chambers have floors
recessed three meters down, with ribbed, almost
organic girders running from side to side. Within the
recess, a layer of mist, two meters deep, casts a sheen
across the whole room, catching the ambient blue
glow and making a beam that lies across it. Beneath
the beam, in the mist, rest hundreds of withered but
serene Engineer bodies, laid out in disciplined rows.
If the PCs touch the mist they receive a mild electric
shock from it, and a gentle musical note from nowhere
plays out across the chamber.
The mist is thick and sweet smelling, but any PC
submerged within it suffers from Severe hypoxia (page
91). An OBSERVATION roll will allow the PCs to con-
clude this is what killed the Engineers, and—by the way
they are set out—they willingly took their own lives.B O M B B AY : The floor of this chamber is an open

goo—the 26 Draconis strain. They are out of reach, but
it is possible to knock one loose—the PCs will need
to use their imagination to get to one. Once loose
the ampule will fall into the central pit. Roll a Stress
the ampule shatters splattering black goo.

THE 26 DRACONIS STRAIN
If a PC becomes infected by the black goo or through the touch of an Abomination, they are in deep shit.
The only chance they have is to ingest or inject another dose of the 26 Draconis strain. If they do this, they
still have little hope. They must make a STAMINA roll, and then add the number of
to a D6 roll:
1–4The PC feels strong for a moment, but it’s a false hope. The black goo starts a rapid conversion of
their DNA. Their bodies bubble and burst in a welter of black gore. They die. All who witness this
gain +1 STRESS LEVEL .
5The PC convulses for three Rounds as the black goo accelerates the transformation—then they
immediately evolve into the next stage of Abomination. All who witness this gain +1 STRESS LEVEL
and must make an immediate Panic Roll.
6The infection is slowed but not cured. The PC will feel better, but their doom is still assured. How-
ever, the infection is dormant for four Shifts, but then continues to consume the PC as normal.
7+The infection is halted, and the PC will survive. However, they have forever been tainted by the 26
Draconis strain—how will this affect them in the future?

AZAD R U KMINI
SECURITY OFFICER, UNCSS TYPHOON
Frightened and pessimistic but not willing to go down
without a fight, Rukmini has refused to join the Per-
fected. He has been given time to reconsider his deci-
sion. He doesn’t know where Barton and Shields are. He
will risk his life to save the PCs, given the chance.

G RÁIN N E S HIELDS
COUNSELOR, UNCSS TYPHOON AND STAGE I
PATHOGEN CARRIER
Resolute, stubborn and ready to die to stop the
Perfected, Shields has pretended to go along with
them. She can feel the infection within her and knows
it can’t be good. When the Perfected were playing
the Navigation Orrery she secretly recorded it on a
data pad she has hidden within her suit. She will pass
the data pad to a PC (this is the fifth campaign clue)
and create a diversion to allow them to escape. She
doesn’t realize this, but in passing the data pad on,
the PC receiving it must resist the infection (Virulence
6) she—as a Pathogen Carrier—unknowingly is con-
taminated with it.

UPPER LEVEL
S TA S I S C H A M B E R : A darkened room with row
upon row of Engineer cryosleep beds, across the
floor and running up the walls. They are all empty.
A C C E S S C H A M B E R : Tunnels in the floor of
this otherwise spartan room lead down into Cargo
1 on the lower level. If a PC is running through
this space, they must make an OBSERVATION roll
to spot and avoid the tunnels. If they fail, they
tumble through, suffering five points of damage
on a MOBILITY roll. They
reduced by one per
end up under the mist in Cargo 1.
THE PERFECTED ENGINEERS
The two Perfected in this place are Engineers that
were infected millennia ago and were two of the
very few Engineers to succumb to Perfection rather
than face annihilation. They are titanic parodies of
their former selves, their black eyes now mottled
and dull, their bodies no longer whiter than white,
crisscrossed with gray biomechanical tubules that
bulge and twist around them—but they are still
recognizable as what they once were.
243G A M E
M O T H E R
S E C T I O N
T H E C H O R I S T R Y : Rows of concentric terraces
lead down to a recessed stage in the center of the
chamber. On this stand rest a weird variety of gongs,
pipes, and cymbals with various mallets for striking. If
one is played the melodious sound echoes around the
ship time and again. The music is so melodious that
playing one of these causes the Engineer Perfected to
momentarily remember their former lives, and pause
for a full Round, taking no action.
S A C R E D C H A M B E R : This chamber appears fea-
tureless and empty until the PCs look up. The ceiling
is the Sistine Chapel in hell. Carved figures writhe
in terror or agony, beastly talons and jaws strain to
tear themselves free from the hull and fall upon the
unwary. It’s such a sight that all viewing it gain +1
STRESS LEVEL .
S T E A M R O O M S : Filled with mist and steam, visibil-
ity in these chambers is reduced to SHORT range. They
are also hot—for every Round after the first in here the
PCs suffer heatstroke (page 91).
P OW E R C H A M B E R S A N D D R I V E C H A M B E R :
Ornate structures weave and wrap around these
rooms, and hum with restrained energy.
V I E W I N G R O O M : The two Engineer Perfected are
here, using their telepathic abilities to monitor the PCs’
progress through the Juggernaut. Once the PCs have
delved deep enough into the ship—and at a time of
your choosing to best enhance the excitement—they
will act. See the event Join Us. Part of the ship’s struc-
ture has decayed away, and the Perfected can access
the atrium cavern or the Navigator Orrery from here.
N AV I G AT O R O R R E R Y : The chamber is dominated
by the raised navigation dais in the center of the room
and the orrery holograms that swirl and dance above it.
Central to this display is a mottled gas giant orbited by
a four-sided, almost circular structure, with an immense
outer ring connected to a central hub by spiraling
booms. The outer ring has four great hangars, and the
central hub is a massive flattened sphere seemingly
fashioned by the hands of the gods themselves. It spins
in breathtakingly elegant laziness. It is the Lychgate.
This is the fifth campaign clue (page 162).

EVENTS
D O N ’ T I G N O R E T H E J O E S : Shortly after the
PCs have boarded the UNCSS Typhoon, they will be
met by the ship’s Working Joes—Jake and Elwood.
They challenge the PCs, saying they are unauthorized
personnel and must leave the ship immediately. They
will follow the PCs, repeating this challenge, and—if
the PCs do not leave—will wait for a suitable moment,
then attack the intruders.
S H I E L D I N G H E R F R I E N D S : Once the PCs have
entered the Engineer Juggernaut and made enough
noise to alert those already inside to their presence,
Gráinne Shields acts. She knows the PCs are walking
into danger. She shouts a warning and tries to reach
them, although a nearby Deacon will attempt to stop
her. She will fight to reach them and hand over her
data pad.
T H E T R A I T O R : While the PCs are inside the Engi-
neer Juggernaut, Leland Barton approaches them or
allows himself to be found and rescued. However, it is
a ruse. He wants to gain the PCs’ trust and help them
escape, so he can take over the Solovetsky Island and
bring it here for the Perfected. Despite his infection he
still looks human, albeit a little unwell. He will pass it
off as the stress of the situation. A successful MEDICAL
FINALE
Once the PCs reject the Perfected’s offer to join
them (above), the Perfected have every intention
of letting at least one escape, but capturing or kill-
ing some of the others, to make the escape look
genuine. Both Perfected will chase them down,
along with Mother Ma’Kayla, four devotees, and
three Deacons, using telepathy and voiced shouts
of: “You cannot escape, submit to perfection!”
They will try to trap the PCs, shepherding them
through the Juggernaut but eventually allowing
them to escape.
But it will be a tough chase, and not every PC
may make it out alive.
AID roll will diagnose he is suffering from the Abomi-
nation pathogen, and he is highly infectious. If at any
point a PC mentions Barton’s wife and that she is alive
he will break down, and—if the PCs succeed at an
opposed MANIPULATION roll—tell them the truth. He
will then do all he can to help them escape.
S TA L K I N G D E A C O N : As the PCs explore the
Engineer Juggernaut, a Deacon is nearby. It does not
intend to attack, but is tracking the PCs’ movements,
so they can be trapped at the right moment. Enter
stealth mode.
J O I N U S : The Perfected move to intercept the PCs,
sending a telepathic wave of positive emotion and
images of warmth and satisfaction. The PCs’ minds
are flooded with images of love, togetherness, and
the wonder of the universe alongside images of being
trapped. They say: “Join us and experience Perfection.
There is nowhere to run to, and no way out. Gift us
your ship and you will be honored among us.” The PCs
must make an Empathy test, attribute only—if they fail,
they must make an immediate Panic Roll, if they suc-
ceed they gain +1 STRESS LEVEL . The Perfected start
the hunt for the PCs, sending Mother Ma’Kayla, her
devotees and three Deacons to track them down.
EPILOGUE
The coordinates data for the Lychgate will take
time for DA/UT/UR to decode. How long will
depend on where in the campaign you run this
expedition. The coordinates should become avail-
able at the end of the campaign, to allow the PCs
to race to the Lychgate for the campaign finale.
Following this story, the PCs could recommend
and be involved in the colonization of Azizo, or
advocate for the destruction of Arzu using the
UNCSS Ìyánlá’s stocks of terraforming nukes. ■

METAPUZZLE CLUE #5—INTERPRETATION OF THE HOLOGRAM ORRERY
The Engineer structure—the Lychgate—orbits a super gas giant. The Orrery data provides spatial
coordinates but to decode, analyze and identify where the data refers to will require the
processing power of DA/UT/UR aboard Solovetsky Island.
Arzu, the moon of KOI-2702.07, the gas giant called Palmyra, is highlighted on the Orrery. An
interstellar trajectory between it and the Lychgate has been calculated and overlaid on the
projection.
Engineer hieroglyphs float within the stars and systems. Translation:
—THE LYCHGATE IS OUR HOPE OF A FUTURE—ITS LOCATION TO BE PROTECTED FROM OUR CHILDREN—ACCESS TO
THIS INFORMATION MUST BE WITHHELD—

L E T S L E E P I N G
G O D S L I E
“If you do not enter the tiger’s
cave you will not catch its cub.”
— J A PA N E S E P R OV E R B
The PCs are sent to survey Pelican Colony, and find
a planet swept clean of life by radiation. They also
detect the smoking wreckage of a crashed spaceship.
The colony is kept operational by primitive automatons,
little more than automated Powerloaders with no
resemblance to androids or synthetics, that view the
PCs as a problem that needs cleaning up. They learn
that the survivors from the crashed ship are the pirates,
Gorham’s Marauders, here to destroy the Perfected.
Mounting a mission into the bowels of an ancient Engi-
neer Guardian ship they uncover the terrifying truth
and find themselves in a desperate race to not only
survive, but to stop the horrors they have unearthed.
W H AT I S G O I N G O N ?
Pelican Colony KOI-947.01 was a flourishing agri-
cultural society—the “breadbasket of the frontier”—
boasting a population in the millions in 2100. Although
the colony survived the Isolation, it shrank to one city
246
of 100,000. Then, a year ago, disaster struck. The local
sun, a gentle G7 main sequence yellow star, turned
angry, flooding the system with radiation. Pelican
Colony became uninhabitable overnight.1 0 .
A few people managed to escape the planet, while
some took refuge in the tunnels behind the great
Godafoss waterfall or in the Skritio Caves, an ancient
Engineer Guardian ship that’s been lying in the moun-
tains so long it has merged with the landscape. All the
rest died, their irradiated bodies still lying where they
fell, macabre statues to a once flourishing city. Those
who fled into the tunnels behind the Godafoss water-
fall eventually starved to death. Those who fled to the
perceived safety of the Skritio Caves were saved from
the radiation but stumbled across the slumbering Per-
fected that inhabit the ship, and the 26 Draconis strain.
They were infected. Most died hideous deaths, but
some survived. They lie, sleeping within the bowels of
the vessel, in altered states of Abomination.
Since then, the colony’s automatons have con-
tinued to work without missing a beat—facilities are
well-maintained, streets are clean, fields are tended,
although little grows in the radiation.
J.V.Gorham, the leader of Gorham’s Marauders,
traveled to Pelican Colony to check out information
she extracted from a captured devotee of the Children
WHAT’S THE STORY, MOTHER?
The PCs receive a video call from Gaius aboard
UNCSS Ìyánlá
Ìyánlá..
“Your next assignment, Solovetsky Island, is
Pelican Colony KOI-947.01. It is an agricultural set-
tlement that used to provide significant imports
of food into the Middle Heavens before the
Isolation. The environment is fertile and climate
temperate, average daytime temperature a balmy
24°C. Established by the Weyland Corporation in
2049, Pelican came under the Three World Empire
later in the century. Population in 2100 reported
to be 6.5 million. And it’s big. Gravity of 1.5G and a
diurnal duration of 48 hours.

of the Two Divines—that Perfected exist in a cave
in the mountains near the city. In her pirate vessel,
the Spirit of Trafalgar, she encountered a ship of the
Children of the Two Divines and chased it into orbit.
However, the Spirit of Trafalgar suffered a catastrophic
mechanical failure—in fact sabotage by her traitorous
crew member, Nessa Majken—and the ship crashed
south of the city. Five of the crew were killed in the
crash, but Gorham and four others, Rashid Ravindra,
Martina Willamar, Dijana Klaasen and Majken, sur-

computers, but Majken took a secret copy of the data
to pass to the Perfected. They headed into the city,
finding refuge in the Godafoss Caverns.
24 hours later, Gorham and Majken left their injured
crewmates at the Godafoss refuge and traveled to the
Extrasolar Colonial Administration Center to figure
out how to send a distress beacon. Majken convinced
Gorham, against her better judgment, to reconnoiter
the Skritio Caves. When they find what they are look-
ing for, Majken intends to betray Gorham and hand her,
and the navigation data, to the Perfected.
As usual, you will operate under the initial
survey and assessment responsibilities of the
Great Mother Mission. You will need to establish
contact with the local authorities, should they
exist, and offer assistance. Naturally, your Colony
Potential Report should focus on the future
farming opportunities and how soon imports back
home can resume, but also scientific research
possibilities and the usual ad hoc opportunities
that may arise.
Good luck, Solovetsky Island.”
C L U E S T O T H E M E TA P U Z Z L E
The PCs can learn the sixth campaign clue (page
162) by exploring the Guardian ship and translating
the Engineer glyphs in the Shrine. They can also
corroborate the first campaign clue (page 162) by
checking the Spirit of Trafalgar’s logs and seeing that
its navigation data has been wiped, or by rescuing and
talking to J.V. Gorham.

SOLAR SYSTEM
& COLONY RECORD
KOI-947 System and KOI-947.01
KOI-947.01
The planet is scorchingly hot, exceeding 40 °C with
potential for heatstroke for careless PCs (page
91). The land is prone to wildfires and firenadoes
fanned by the winds. It’s a big planet too, with a
surface gravity of 1.5G, resulting in gravity dyspraxia
(page 91) and a day that’s 48 hours long. But
the biggest problem is the radiation. At all times on
KOI-947.01 the PCs will suffer the effects of Weak
radiation, unless they are protected by a sealed com-
pression suit (don’t forget their Air Supply rolls), are
inside their ship or a vehicle, in the Godafoss caverns
or the Guardian ship. The local star is unpredictable,
and at any time Pelican Colony can be swept with a
radiation storm (see the event Bring Me Sunshine).
The planetary map gives you all the details
you need for KOI-947.01 should your PCs want to
further explore or even colonize it, using the rules
in the Appendix: Building Your Own Better World
(page 275).

E X P E D I T I O N S
KICKING OFF THE ACTION
The action starts as the PCs arrive in the KOI-947
system. The PCs immediately detect the activity of the
host star and the high levels of radiation it’s kicking
out, a bad portent for Pelican Colony.
Pelican Colony is built in the steep foothills of the
mountains, a beautiful sight—two great rivers ride
down from the heights and split into what was once
a lush and fertile delta. Stunning waterfalls create a
spray that leaves the colony with almost permanent
rainbows, culminating in the glory of the Godafoss
falls, right in the center of the city. From a distance,
Pelican Colony looks fully functioning, clean streets
brightly illuminated, well-maintained buildings gleam-
ing in the sun and machines working the fields.
But on closer inspection the PCs notice the
following:
There is a complete absence of life, and an absence
of radio or other transmissions you would expect
from a functioning society.
There are no cloud formations, the sunlight is very
bright, and the planet looks arid.
The surface temperature is above 40°C and is
bathed in Weak radiation.
And they detect a weak transponder beacon from a
recent crash site, to the south of the city.

O N A P P R O A C H : Once the PCs start their approach
to the city, they receive an automatic beacon, signal-
ing them to land at the spaceport. If they ignore this
THE AUTOMATONS
Pelican Colony is entirely automated, the farms,
factories and utilities all running themselves. Other
activities are carried out by the automatons, little more
than automated Powerloaders. Their programming is
simple—fulfill basic tasks and protect life. They will
also protect themselves against being deactivated, as
they must be active to succeed in their primary tasks.
To deactivate an automaton a PC needs to access the
control panel on its back, using MOBILITY to climb up
the hand and footholds built into the machine for that
purpose, and make a COMTECH roll. The automatons
will use force to protect the PCs, from the radiation or
and choose to land somewhere other than the space-
port they will receive these sequential messages from
the spaceport’s automated Traffic Control, increasing
in urgency with each message:
“You are diverting from your allocated course.
Please resume your course for the safety of all traffic.”
“You are not on your allotted course. Do you require
assistance?”
“Emergency assistance is en route to your position.
Please wait. Help will be with you soon.”
If the PCs say they are landing elsewhere the auto-
mated system won’t understand, and will respond:
“Landing is only permitted at the spaceport. Any diver-
sion implies mechanical failure or other emergency
and danger to your lives.”
L A N D I N G : Landing requires a PILOT test. If the roll
is failed, the ship has landed heavily and takes D3
damage. Wherever they land, they will be met by D6
automatons one Turn after they have touched down.
The automatons have been sent to rescue the PCs,
thinking they have landed here due to malfunction or
misfortune.
S H O R E PA R T Y : As there is a crashed ship, Lakota
Monroe (page 157) suggests they should see if
anyone needs help, and that she should join the shore
party as a medic.
other threats as the robots see it, using the automaton
attack table.

A NOTE FROM MU/TH/UR: These machines take half damage (rounding up)
from fire and are immune to radiation and EMP effects. If they are
attacked, or someone attempts to deactivate them, they will defend

hits the target is grappled and will be taken to Godafoss falls or another safe location.

INTIMIDATE: The automaton produces a low growl and takes a step forward. It says: “For your safety, obey my
instructions—you have five seconds to comply.” The target gains +1 STRESS LEVEL and all future automaton
attack rolls for this robot gain +1 to the roll.
5
KNOCK: The automaton sweeps its huge arms at the target and attacks with eight Base Dice. If the target is
hit, they only take one point of damage, are knocked prone and must make a STAMINA roll or be stunned,
losing their next slow action.

7SEARING FLAME: In an attempt to frighten the target using its cutting torch the automaton actually makes an

attack has three Base Dice, Damage 1.
9
CRUSH: The automaton seeks to immobilize the target as swiftly as possible, deeming it a safety threat. It
grabs with the grip-vice and crushes without mercy, with a ten Base Dice attack, Damage 1. If the target takes
any damage they have been crushed in half, and are killed. All who witness this gain +1 STRESS LEVEL and
must make a Panic Roll.

E X P E D I T I O N S
P I R AT E V E S S E L S P I R I T O F T R A FA L G A R
The PCs recognize this ship as an old Corvus-class
vessel and see its registration number and name. A
check of their ship’s records will reveal it was launched
in 2088 under the name USCSS Borys. It’s being
stripped down and salvaged by ten automatons, piling
the remains into automated trucks for return to scrap
yards. There is no sign of the crew. The automatons
will ignore the PCs until, after one Turn, three make
their way to UNCSS Solovetsky Island and start the
work to salvage it (see the event Clean Up Crews). If
the PCs interfere with the automatons, they will stop
salvaging and focus on protecting the PCs from the
radiation and themselves, by taking them, by force if
necessary, to the Godafoss Refuge for their own safety.
If the PCs attempt to board the Spirit of Trafalgar,
an automaton will try to stop them “for their own
safety.” But once aboard, the PCs can reach the
remains of the bridge and check the logs. This will
show them the details of the chase and the engine fail-
ure that led to the crash, and that the ship’s navigation
data was wiped from the computer after the attack
(and learn the conclusions of the first campaign clue).
A successful COMTECH roll shows them that the data
was also downloaded at the moment it was wiped.
As the PCs watch the automatons salvaging the
ship a human figure is revealed from the wreckage.
An automaton almost lovingly places the body in a
coffin-sized metal container, then picks it up between
its grip vices and walks the five kilometers to the
Godafoss refuge, where it places the body alongside
four other coffins. The victim is the Spirit of Trafalgar’s
pilot, Adam Ingram. He is dead.

E X P E D I T I O N S
PELICAN COLONY
S PA C E P O R T : Fully automated and in good working
order, D6 automatons are always in close proximity to a
landed ship. This is the only place in the colony where
the automatons won’t try to salvage a vessel (see the
event Clean Up Crews).
A D M I N I S T R AT I O N C E N T E R : A two-story office
block with a viewing tower housing the Colonial Oper-
ations control center. There is a desiccated body here,
wearing a uniform with the name tag: “Lohengrin.”
The colony command logs and the long data disc are
found here. If the PCs spend a Turn analyzing the disc,
they can learn the following:
Population of five million in 2110. In the years imme-
diately afterwards, there was terrible civil turmoil,
and many died or fled the planet.
In the years between 2120 and 2140, other colonies
launched raids on Pelican Colony, to capture food
supplies and production. The wars that followed
killed many. Population in 2150 was 100,000.
Stability restored, Pelican Colony looked after itself.
Trade with other colonies was banned.
In 2183 the local star became unstable, followed in
2184 by sudden radiation storms.
2185 population 0.
The PCs can also access the last three log entries,
two from 36 hours ago, and one from 10 months.
See the adjacent sidebar.

3 W E A D M I N I S T R AT I O N : This four-story building
was the center of the 3WE’s administration and oper-
ations, and as such houses the Colonial Operations
Control Room.
U N I V E R S I T Y : The facility is a sweeping but
deserted campus. An automated registrar will
welcome them and ask which courses they are
considering.
H O P P I P O L L A L A K E & D A M : A huge hydro-elec-
tric facility built within the folds of the mountains. A
small army of automatons keeps it maintained.
R E S I D E N T I A L Z O N E S : These would be perfect
places to live, except for the scorching radiation.
FA R M FA C T O R Y Z O N E S : Buzzing with robotic
activity, these places are running flat out to feed and
support a population that’s long since gone.
L E I S U R E Z O N E S : Parks, malls, sports facilities,
and nightlife centers are all ready for people to kill
time on their off days, including a fully operational
theme park with roller coasters, log flumes and a giant
Ferris wheel.

FINDING THE REFUGE
There are four ways the PCs can learn of the
refuge beneath the Godafoss falls: an automaton
may capture a PC and take them there for their
safety; they can follow an automaton as it returns
a victim of the crash to the refuge; they can access
the logs at the Administration Building; and they
can find and examine the remains of the survivor
camp within the Guardian ship.
253G A M E
M O T H E R
S E C T I O N
BREAKING AND ENTERING
The PCs cannot access any buildings in the city, as
automated systems will deny them entry. To hack in
requires an opposed COMTECH roll versus eight Base
Dice. Whatever the outcome of the roll, an autom-
aton will appear after D6 Rounds to investigate. If
hacking doesn’t work, the PCs can break the door
down or smash a window with a STAMINA roll, but
again an automaton will arrive in D6 Rounds to
repair the damage and protect the PCs from their
own hazardous behavior, by restraining them.
GODAFOSS
Godafoss falls is a wonderful sweeping cres-
cent-shaped waterfall, 300 meters wide and 100
meters high—a local beauty spot. Roads and walkways
lead down to the river below. One of these forms a
wide rocky shelf that goes behind the falls themselves.
This leads to the Godafoss Caverns.
C AV E R N S : The caverns are deep and adorned
with semi-transparent stalactites and stalagmites, all
illuminated with tastefully placed lighting to enhance
the ambiance. The entrance tunnel goes 200 meters
before opening into a wide cavern full of equipment,
wires, cables and 150 dead bodies—survivors who
starved to death, now just bones and rags. There are
five coffins here, containing the dead crew of the
Spirit of Trafalgar, and three survivors: Rashid Ravin-
dra, Martina Willamar, and Dijana Klaassen. Unless
the PCs actively sneak into the caverns, they will
assume the PCs are Children of the Two Divines, from
the ship they had been chasing. They lay an ambush
and will attack when the PCs enter the room. Enter
stealth mode.
If the PCs subdue the Marauders through violence,
they will be defiant in defeat—they will not cooperate
or answer any questions. In this case, a communicator
crackles and the PCs hear the following message:
“We’ve arrived at the ECA ops room and can’t find a
way to send a distress beacon, so we’ll have to think
again. Majken has convinced me we should take a look
at those caves we came for, by the dam, although it’s
risky with only the two of us. I’ll call in again in three
hours. Gorham out.” If the PCs ended the confron-
tation peacefully and convinced the Marauders they
are friendly, they will help the PCs and offer them this
information, as well as details of the Marauders’ rea-
sons for opposing the Perfected.
RAS HID RAVIND RA
Single-minded, determined and stoic, Ravindra has
been a loyal follower of J.V. Gorham since the late
days of her grandfather. He has seen much death and
heartbreak and is determined to see the end of the
Perfected and the Children of the Two Divines. Despite
his injuries from the crash, he will not surrender and
any attempt to convince him to, has a −2 modification.

E X P E D I T I O N S
MARTINA WILLAMAR
Headstrong, athletic, and tough, Willamar is a
notorious security officer in the Marauders’ circles
known for her take-no-prisoners approach to her
enemies. She grew up with the young J.V. Gorham and
is intensely loyal to her. She intends to fight to the
death—any attempt to convince her to surrender has a
−2 modification.
STRENGTH 4, AGILITY 5, WITS 3, EMPATHY 3
HEALTH: 4
SKILLS: Close Combat 2, Stamina 1, Observation 1,
Medical Aid 1, Command 2, Mobility 2, Ranged
Combat 3

E-7 Shockgun with KIP rounds, incinerator unit (2
reloads), Electroshock grenades
DIJANA KLAASS EN
Reasonable, fair-minded, and conscientious, Klaassen
is an engineering genius. She hates conflict but
realizes the Perfected are an existential threat,
although she believes that the devotees of the
Children of the Two Divines must have been brain-
washed and are victims too—they deserve a chance to
be saved. She will fight to defend herself if she has to,
but always prefers peaceful resolutions.

S E C T I O N
THE WHISPERING GALLERY
The bulbous head of the Engineer ship has been
designed to channel and amplify sound. It’s
not only hard to place the location of any given
noise—it might be hundreds of meters away, but
you’d swear it was whispering in your ear, or
something close echoes as if it were far off—the
structure is also designed to amplify it. A scream,
a gunshot or explosion immediately fills the
ship’s empty spaces with booming noise that
builds on itself before seeping away. Everyone
aboard the vessel who hears this for the first time
gains +1 STRESS LEVEL and must make a STAMINA
roll or spend a Round holding their ears against
the onslaught.
THE GUARDIAN
This ship, an elegantly elongated horseshoe with
a giant bulbous head to one side, measures 1,000
meters from top to tip, the head itself nearly 400
meters across and 600 meters long. It crashed on
this planet millennia ago and the world has grown
over and around it. A small part of one side of the
head is all that remains visible, now a part of the
mountains. The interior has been molded by time and
the pressure of mountains growing around—its layout
bears little similarity to any other Guardian ship that
may still exist in the universe. The vessel will never fly
again, but power still hums. The inside is bathed in an
eerie blue glow—just bright enough to see, not bright
enough to dispel the shadows.
The interior of the vessel is cool, with breathable
air, and protects against the planetary radiation. The
walls and floors look almost carved in a dull obsidian
that swallows the light and prevents any comms in or
out. In places, it seems the structure has been twisted
by some irresistible force. Sounds echo upon them-
selves, a noise in one part of the ship is channeled
and heard in another, hundreds of meters away. Just
stepping aboard this vessel for the first time is so
awe-inspiring that all PCs gain +1 STRESS LEVEL .
E N T R A N C E S : Oval openings in the side of the ship
can be reached by climbing up sloped gravel-strewn
ground. The incline is too steep for a vehicle, and
climbing in is not straight-forward. A successful
MOBILITY roll is required to avoid sliding back down
with a rush of stones.
C AV E R N O U S C H A M B E R S : Enormous, misshapen,
and twisted, with deep shadows. From the twisted
portico entrance the PCs can see the chamber opens
into a huge nave, with ribbed surfaces covered in
undisturbed dust and debris. A distant drip of water
can be heard.
In one of these chambers, the PCs come across
scuffed footprints in the dust. If they follow the trail,
they reach a darkened corner to find a survivor. He
seems almost normal, although his arms are a bit
25 6
misshapen—he is a Stage II Mutated Abomination
(page 123). He begs for forgiveness and for mercy
(without saying what for), and to be killed. He will
become distraught and attack them within five
Rounds if the PCs don’t do something to prevent it.
H E A D S : These chambers are filled with a forest of
tall Engineer head statues, with less than five meters
between each. There are hundreds, so many in fact
that it’s ridiculously easy to get lost amongst them,
especially given the echoes that make following the
sound of someone’s voice almost impossible. Each PC
must make an OBSERVATION test with a −3 modifica-
tion or they will get lost amongst them. Any PC who
gets lost must make a Panic Roll.
N AV I G AT I O N O R R E R Y : A huge chamber with a
raised dais in the middle and an unoccupied Engineer
navigator’s chair. Nothing responds to the PCs’ touch.
An intense blue glow can be seen coming from the
adjoining Power chamber.
P O W E R : Dominating this space, set into the floor
like an electric wound, is a five-meter-wide gash glow-
ing an intense electric blue, spitting sparks into the
ozone-filled air. Almost too bright to look at directly,
the gash has dozens of smaller offshoots branching
in every direction. Any item that uses power is fully
recharged just by being brought within SHORT range
of the gash—the PCs will notice the items getting hot.
A COMTECH roll will identify these as power conduits
feeding the entire structure but saturated with power
and highly unstable. If a point of power from a Power
Supply, or a weapon or tool, is discharged into the
gash the whole network shivers and sparks fly—the
PCs can see how close to catastrophically overloading
the system is. If a grenade or explosive charge is
detonated on it or it is overloaded by connecting a
power generator to it with a HEAVY MACHINERY roll,
a feedback loop is created that will cause the whole
ship to self-destruct in one Turn (see the sidebar The
End of the Ancient Mariner).1 0 .
